<script>
        // Micro-interaction for cards
        document.querySelectorAll('.group.cursor-pointer').forEach(card => {
            card.addEventListener('mousedown', () => card.style.transform = 'scale(0.98)');
            card.addEventListener('mouseup', () => card.style.transform = 'scale(1)');
            card.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => card.style.transform = 'scale(1)');
        });

        // Simple real-time update simulator for the "Active Field Staff"
        setInterval(() => {
            const staffCount = document.querySelector('span.text-primary.font-headline-md');
            if(staffCount && staffCount.innerText == '124.5') return; // Target first one by accident? No, let's targeting specifically
            // Find the 48
            const counters = document.querySelectorAll('.font-headline-md');
            counters.forEach(c => {
                if(c.innerText === '48') {
                    const change = Math.random() > 0.5 ? 1 : -1;
                    const newVal = Math.max(40, Math.min(60, parseInt(c.innerText) + change));
                    c.innerText = newVal;
                }
            });
        }, 5000);
    </script>

<script>
        // Simple micro-interaction for the More button to toggle drawer
        const moreBtn = document.querySelector('nav div:last-child');
        const drawer = document.getElementById('nav-drawer');
        const overlay = document.getElementById('drawer-overlay');

        moreBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
            drawer.classList.remove('translate-x-[-100%]');
            overlay.classList.remove('opacity-0', 'pointer-events-none');
        });

        overlay.addEventListener('click', () => {
            drawer.classList.add('translate-x-[-100%]');
            overlay.classList.add('opacity-0', 'pointer-events-none');
        });
    </script>

        // Micro-interactions and subtle effects
        document.querySelectorAll('tr').forEach(row => {
            row.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => {
                row.style.transform = 'translateX(4px)';
                row.style.transition = 'transform 0.2s ease-out';
            });
            row.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => {
                row.style.transform = 'translateX(0)';
            });
        });

        // Toggle Active State Simulation
        const navItems = document.querySelectorAll('nav a');
        navItems.forEach(item => {
            item.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
                // Not actually navigating, just UI feedback
                navItems.forEach(ni => {
                    ni.classList.remove('bg-secondary-container', 'text-on-secondary-container', 'rounded-full', 'px-4', 'py-1');
                    ni.classList.add('text-on-surface-variant', 'p-2');
                    const span = ni.querySelector('.material-symbols-outlined');
                    if(span) span.style.fontVariationSettings = "'FILL' 0";
                });
                item.classList.remove('text-on-surface-variant', 'p-2');
                item.classList.add('bg-secondary-container', 'text-on-secondary-container', 'rounded-full', 'px-4', 'py-1');
                const span = item.querySelector('.material-symbols-outlined');
                if(span) span.style.fontVariationSettings = "'FILL' 1";
            });
        });
    </script>

        // Micro-interactions for the facility map
        document.querySelectorAll('.zone-card').forEach(card => {
            card.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => {
                const zoneId = card.id.replace('zone-', '');
                console.log(`Hovering over ${zoneId}`);
                // Highlight logic can be expanded here
            });
            
            card.addEventListener('click', () => {
                const zoneId = card.id.replace('zone-', '');
                alert(`Redirecting to detailed telemetry for ${zoneId.toUpperCase()} zone...`);
            });
        });

        // Simulating machinery status updates
        setInterval(() => {
            const productionDot = document.querySelector('.status-pulse[title="Crusher Malfunction"]');
            if(productionDot) {
                productionDot.classList.toggle('opacity-50');
            }
        }, 1000);
    </script>

<script>
        // Micro-interaction for hover effects and dynamic updates
        document.querySelectorAll('.bento-card').forEach(card => {
            card.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => {
                card.style.transform = 'translateY(-2px)';
                card.style.transition = 'transform 0.2s ease-out';
            });
            card.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => {
                card.style.transform = 'translateY(0px)';
            });
        });

        // Atmospheric fade-in for charts
        window.addEventListener('load', () => {
            const chartBars = document.querySelectorAll('.bg-primary, .bg-secondary, .bg-tertiary-container');
            chartBars.forEach(bar => {
                const finalWidth = bar.style.width;
                bar.style.width = '0%';
                setTimeout(() => {
                    bar.style.transition = 'width 1s cubic-bezier(0.175, 0.885, 0.32, 1.275)';
                    bar.style.width = finalWidth;
                }, 300);
            });
        });
    </script>

<script>
        // Simple micro-interaction for chart animation
        window.addEventListener('load', () => {
            const bars = document.querySelectorAll('.chart-bar');
            bars.forEach(bar => {
                const height = bar.style.height;
                bar.style.height = '0%';
                setTimeout(() => {
                    bar.style.height = height;
                }, 100);
            });
        });
    </script>

        // Simple micro-interaction for measurement input
        const weightInput = document.querySelector('input[type="number"]');
        if (weightInput) {
            weightInput.addEventListener('input', (e) => {
                if (e.target.value > 200) {
                    e.target.classList.add('text-error', 'border-error');
                } else {
                    e.target.classList.remove('text-error', 'border-error');
                }
            });
        }

        // Simulating collection status update
        const tableRows = document.querySelectorAll('tbody tr');
        tableRows.forEach(row => {
            row.addEventListener('click', () => {
                row.classList.toggle('bg-primary-fixed-dim');
                row.classList.toggle('bg-opacity-10');
            });
        });
    </script>

<script>
        // Simple search interactivity
        document.querySelector('input[type="text"]').addEventListener('input', function(e) {
            const term = e.target.value.toLowerCase();
            const rows = document.querySelectorAll('tbody tr');
            rows.forEach(row => {
                const text = row.textContent.toLowerCase();
                row.style.display = text.includes(term) ? '' : 'none';
            });
        });

        // Hover effects for the grid items
        const bentoItems = document.querySelectorAll('.bento-grid > section');
        bentoItems.forEach(item => {
            item.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => {
                item.style.transform = 'translateY(-2px)';
                item.style.transition = 'all 0.3s ease';
            });
            item.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => {
                item.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
            });
        });
    </script>

<script>
    const moreBtn = document.querySelector('nav div:last-child');
    const drawer = document.getElementById('nav-drawer');
    const overlay = document.getElementById('drawer-overlay');

    moreBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        drawer.classList.remove('translate-x-[-100%]');
        overlay.classList.remove('opacity-0', 'pointer-events-none');
    });

    overlay.addEventListener('click', () => {
        drawer.classList.add('translate-x-[-100%]');
        overlay.classList.add('opacity-0', 'pointer-events-none');
    });
</script>
